  azimuth_micro_t2_sight (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.attachments.ALPHA.universal.azimuth_t_series.azimuth_micro_t2_sight
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    --- END CODE ---
  runtime_properties (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.attachments.ALPHA.universal.azimuth_t_series.azimuth_micro_t2_sight.runtime_properties
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    return {
    	holo_size = 64,
    	brightness = {
    	},
    	cut_model = function(p1) --[[ cut_model | Line: 14 ]]
    		local azimuth_micro_t2_lens_caps = p1:FindFirstChild("azimuth_micro_t2_lens_caps")
    		local azimuth_t2_condura_fabric_wrap = p1:FindFirstChild("azimuth_t2_condura_fabric_wrap")
    		local t = {
    			normal = { p1, azimuth_micro_t2_lens_caps, azimuth_t2_condura_fabric_wrap }
    		}
    		local t2 = {}
    		local cut_scope = p1:FindFirstChild("cut_scope")
    		local v1 = if azimuth_micro_t2_lens_caps then azimuth_micro_t2_lens_caps:FindFirstChild("cut_scope") else nil
    		local v2 = if azimuth_t2_condura_fabric_wrap then azimuth_t2_condura_fabric_wrap:FindFirstChild("cut_scope") else nil
    		t2[1] = cut_scope
    		t2[2] = v1
    		t2[3] = v2
    		t.cut = t2
    }
    --- END CODE ---

  alistair_ar536_prism_5x_sight (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.attachments.ALPHA.universal.thumbscrew_flattop_mount.alistair_ar536_prism_5x_sight
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    --- END CODE ---
  runtime_properties (ModuleScript)
    Path: game.ReplicatedStorage.attachments.ALPHA.universal.thumbscrew_flattop_mount.alistair_ar536_prism_5x_sight.runtime_properties
    --- DECOMPILED CODE ---
    return {
    	aim_fov = 16,
    	eye_relief_sensitivity = 3.5,
    	brightness = {
    	},
    	cut_model = function(p1) --[[ cut_model | Line: 17 ]]
    		local t = { p1, p1.lens }
    		local t2 = { p1:WaitForChild("cut") }
    		local t3 = {}
    		local t4 = { "top_rail", "left_rail", "right_rail" }
    		for k, v in pairs(p1:GetChildren()) do
    			if table.find(t3, v.Name) or table.find(t4, v.Name) then
    				if not table.find(t4, v.Name) then
    					table.insert(t, v)
    				for k2, v2 in pairs(v:GetDescendants()) do
    					if v2:IsA("MeshPart") and v2.Transparency == 0 then
    						table.insert(t, v2)
    		return {
    			cut = t2
    		}
    }
    --- END CODE ---
